Sesavali

1. 1. sityva `religiis~ gansazRvreba
sityva „religia“ momdinareobs winaqristianuli xanidan,
magram adreuli periodidanve iqca qristianuli enis nawilad.
sityvidan religere („mowiwebiT pativiscema“) „religia“ niSnavs
mokrZalebiTa da sifrTxiliT moekido wmindas (numinose),
zebunebrivi Zalis mqone arsebas, yovelive amqveyniurisgan
(profane) gansxvavebiT.
sxva mniSvnelobiT, religio aris adamianebis SiSnarevi damo­
kidebuleba wminda arsebisadmi. es aris keTilmorwmunis SiSi,
raTa raimeTi ar Seuracxhyos RvTaebrivi arseba(ni). aqedan
gamomdinare zedsarTavma saxelma „religiuri“ _ „morCilis, RvTismoSiSis“ mniSvneloba miiRo.
am ukanaskneli mniSvnelobiT SeiTvisa qristianulma sa­m­
yaromac sityva „religia“. Suasaukuneebis dasavlur (la­
Tinur) qristianobaSi religio aRniSnavs monastrul cxovre­
bas: siRaribes, morCilebas, qorwinebis gareSe cxov­rebas da
gamudmebul locvas. religiousus (religiuri) aRmatebiTi mniS­
vnelobiT niSnavda bers, monazons.
qristianul samyaroSi aseve gavrcelebulia am sityvis ne­
tari avgustineseuli (+430 w.) ganmartebac, romelic sxva
laTini mwerlis, laqtanciusis ganmartebis msgavsad, igi
9

“SeerTebas” niSnavs, Tumca umatebda, rom sityva “religia”
RmerTTan (dakarguli) “kavSiris aRdgenas” niSnavs.
CineTSi religias uwodeben „Ciao“-s, rac niSnavs „moZRvrebas“. indoeTSi sityva „dharma“ gamoxatavs laTinur „reli­
gias“ da niSnavs „wesrigs“. arabulSi ki „din“ aRniSnavs am sit­
yvas (religias) da iTargmneba, rogorc „RvTaebrivi gangeba“.
tradiciulad religias gansazRvraven rogorc rwmenas zeb­
unebrivis mimarT. Tumca arsebobs meore midgomac, romlis
mixedviTac religia es aris Sexedulebebisa da qmedebebis
nebismieri sistema, damaxasiaTebeli adamianis ama Tu im jgu­
fisaTvis, romelic adamianisTvis erTgvar orientirsa Tu
Tayvaniscemisa da msaxurebis obieqts SeiZleba warmoadgen­
des. aqedan gamodis, rom religia es aris nebismieri idealis
Tayvaniscema. magram Tu adamianisTvis ideals warmoadgens
magaliTad fuli da materialuri keTildReoba, maSin Znelia
amgvar damokidebulebas religia daarqva.
ese igi gamodis, rom religia aris rwmena zebunebrivis mi­
marT. magram yvela amgvar rwmenasac ar SeiZleba ewodos re­
ligia, radgan religia unda efuZnebodes sulieri cxovre­
bis umaRles WeSmaritebas, samarTlianobasa da humanurobas.
magaliTad, satanizmi da okultizmi marTalia Seicaven re­
ligiis zogierT elements zebunebrivis mimarT rwmenis CaTv­
liT, magram sinamdvileSi isini religiis damaxinjebisa da
degradaciis produqtebs warmoadgenen.

1. 2. religiis maxasiaTeblebi
RvTis arsebobis faqts SeiZleba sxvadasxva gamoxatuleba
hqondes adamianTa azrovnebaSi Tavisi SinaarsiT, formiT
da sicxadis xarisxiT. religia SeiZleba iyos monoTeisturi
(erTi RmerTis rwmena), poliTeisturi (mravali RmerTis rw­
mena) da dualisturi (ori Tanabari Zalis sulieri sawyisis
aRiareba: keTilisa da borotisa).
religias aqvs ramdenime maxasiaTebeli, romlis gareSec igi
ver iarsebebs, rogorc religia. am SemTxvevaSi igi mxolod
filosofiur da moralur msoflmxedvelobad rCeba.
zogadad aTeizmis1 sapirispirod, pirveli principi religi­
isa gulisxmobs sulieri, srulyofili, gonieri da pirovnu­
li, sawyisis aRiarebas, romelic yovelive arsebulis Semoq­
medi da pirvelmizezia da romelic aqtiurad urTierTobs am
samyarosTan.
religiis meore principis mixedviT, adamians aqvs unari
RmerTTan urTierTobisa. cxovelebisgan gansxvavebiT ada­
miani moazrovne arsebaa da Tan iseTi, romelic acnobier­
ebs rogorc fizikuri sikvdilis, ise maradiuli arsebobis
faqts. msgavsi kategoriebis warmodgenac ki ar SeuZliaT de­
damiwis sxva cocxal arsebebs.
nebismieri religiis damaxasiaTebeli niSania aseve kul­
tis arseboba, anu religiis garegani gamoxatuleba: saR­
vTismsaxuro formebis, sxvadasxva ritualuri moqmedebebisa
da wes-Cveulebebis erToblioba.

1. 3. fsevdoreligiuri sistemebi
a) deizmi
es religiur-filosofiuri mimarTuleba warmoiSva XVII s-is in­
glisSi. deizmi (laT. “deus”, RmerTi) aRiarebs RmerTis arsebo­
bas, magram mas ganixilavs, rogorc am samyarosa da misi kanoneb­
is mxolod Semoqmeds (Semqmnels), sruliad gamoricxavs ra amave
dros yovelgvar gamocxadebas, saswaulebsa da zogadad am sam­
yaroze zrunvas Semoqmedis mxridan. RmerTi samyaros gareT my­
ofobs anu transcendenturia2 anu ar urTierTobs adamianTan.
b) panTeizmi
panTeisturi (berZ. “pan” yvelaferi, “Teos” RmerTi) reli­
giur-filosofiuri swavleba RmerTs aigivebs am samyarosTan,
bunebasTan, adamianTan. panTeizmSi RmerTi ar moiazreba
pirovnul arsebad, romelsac am samyarosgan damoukideblad
arsebobis unari aqvs. igi mTlianad imanenturia3 samyarosi,
kosmosisa, bunebisa, adamianisa. adamianic RvTis nawilad moi­
azreba, romelic (adamiani) droebiT acnobierebs sakuTar
Tavs am qveyniur cxovrebaSi damoukidebel arsebad, Semdeg ki
samudamod SeurTdeba (dainTqmeba, gaibneva) uzenaesi sulis
usazRvro okeaneSi. panTeizmi aseve uaryofs adamianis nebis
Tavisuflebas.
panTeizmi, iseve rogorc deizmi, uaryofs adamianis pirovnul
urTierTobis SesaZleblobas RmerTTan. aseve am mizeziT
isini ar ganixilebian religiebad.

g) Teizmi
Teizmi (berZ. “Teos”, RmerTi), panTeizmisgan gansxvavebiT,
aRiarebs pirovnuli RmerTis arsebobas, xolo deizmisgan
gansxvavebiT, aRiarebs uflis mxridan am samyaroSi Carevis
(masze zrunvis) SesaZleblobasa da aucileblobas. Teisturi
swavlebis mixedviT, RmerTi ara mxolod transcendeturia,
aramed am samyaros imanenturic aris.
Teizmis mniSvnelovan ganmasxvavebel niSnebs warmoadgens
aseve adamianSi Tavisufali nebis arsebobisa da mis mier
RmerTTan urTierTobis unaris aRiarebac. arsebobs sx­
vadasxva Teisturi sistemebi. vinaidan Teizmis ZiriTadi de­
bulebebi saerToa religiuri moZRvrebis principebTan, ami­
tom Tavad religiebsac Teisturi msoflmxedvelobebis rigs
ganukuTvneben.
Tumca Teizmi TavisTavad ar warmoadgens religias, radgan
igi mxolod swavlebad, Teoriebisa da debulebebis er­
Tobliobad rCeba.
d) agnosticizmi
filosofiuri swavlebaa, romelic amtkicebs, rom adamians
ara aqvs unari Seimecnos zebunebrivi samyaro. Sesabamisad,
SeuZleblad miiCneva adamianis mxridan RvTis Semecneba.
swored aqedan momdinareobs am swavlebis saxelwodebac (berZ.
“gnosis” _ Semecneba, a _ uaryofiTi nawilaki). yovelgvari
Semecneba, agnostikosTa azriT, moipoveba adamianis grZno­
baTa organoebis meSveobiT. am mizeziT, Semecnebis obieqti
SeiZleba iyos mxolod is, rac misawvdomia am grZnobebisTvis
anu mxolod grZnobiTi samyaro.

2. warmarToba
sityva warmarTobas ukavSireben laTinur termins paganus,
ro­melic niSnavs “soflis mosaxles, romelmac qristian­
oba ar mi­iRo”. Zveli aRTqmis epoqaSi ebraelebi warmarTebs
uwodebdnen yve­la danarCen ers. am sityvas isini uaryofiTi
mniSvnelobiT iye­nebdnen rogorc zogadad erebis, aseve maTi
religiuri war­modgenebis, moralisa da kulturis misamar­
TiT. iudevelebi ase­ve sityva `goimsac~ iyenebdnen yvela
araiudeveli adamianis mi­sa­marTiT. termini `war­marToba~
iudauri leqsikonidan qri­stianul diskursSic gadmovida,
romelSic igi mxolod re­ligiuri daniSnulebiT ixmareba.
religiaTmcodneebi warmarTul religiebs agreTve po­
liTeistur religiebsac uwodeben, radgan am religiis mim­
devrebi, rogorc wesi, sxvadasxva RvTaebas scemen Tayvans
(aqedan maTi sxva saxelwodebac – kerpTayvanismcemlebi).
monoTeisturi religiebis poziciidan warmarToba ga­
nixileba rogorc ganuviTarebeli da primitiuli xal­
xebisTvis dama­xasiaTebeli movlena. warmarTuli elementebs
SeiZleba wava­wydeT ama Tu im xalxSi gavrcelebuli monoTe­
isturi religiis farglebSic – adaTebsa da wes-CveulebebSi,
xalxur gadmocemebSi, saxviT xelovnebaSi da sxva. am kuTxiT
warmarToba kacobriobis kulturuli memkvidreobis mniS­
vnelovani Semadgeneli nawilia.

2. 1. religiurobis kvali pirvelyofil
sazogadoebaSi
pirvelyofili adamianis cxovrebam mravali arqeologiuri
mowmoba dagvitova sakuTari arsebobis Sesaxeb: Zvlebi, Tavis
qalebi, qvis iaraRebi, dakrZalvis saritualo morTulobe­
bi da qvis kedlebze SemorCenili naxatebi. miuxedavad Cveni
codnis simwirisa am periodis adamianis religiurobis Ses­
axeb, mainc unda davsvaT Semdegi SekiTxva: nuTu homo faber
(mwarmoebeli adamiani), homo sapiens (gonieri adamiani) da
homo ludens (moTamaSe adamiani) ar iyo agreTve homo religiosus
(religiuri adamiani)?
SemorCenili materialuri monacemebi garkveuli war­
modgenebis SeqmnaSi gvexmareba am mimarTulebiT. magaliTad,
sagulisyuroa iaraRis aRqma miTologiasa da religiur cx­
ovrebaSi; aseve legendebi da rwmena-warmodgenebi sivrcis
dapyrobasTan dakavSirebiT; miTologiuri warmodgenebi
SubebTan dakavSirebiT, romlebic mimarTulia cis kamaris
gansagmirad; aseve isrebi, romlebic RrublebSia garWobili.
Tanamedrove velur tomebSi monadireebs miaCniaT, rom cx­
oveli adamians hgavs, magram gamoirCeva uCveulo siZlieriT.
maT sjeraT, rom adamians SeuZlia cxovelad gadaqceva. ami­
tom cxovelis mokvla aResruleba mkacrad dadgenili ritu­
alis mixedviT, amasTan gansakuTrebuli Rirebuleba aqvs
cocxali arsebis Tavis qalasa da Zvlebs.
pirvelyofili adamianis religiurobis mniSvnelovani elements
warmoadgens aseve dakrZalvis simbolikac. yvelaze adreuli
saflavebi TariRdeba Zv. w. 70,000-dan 50,000 wlebs Soris. mi­
wisTvis gardacvlilTa ritualur mibarebas didi mniSvneloba
hqonda cocxlad darCenilTaTvis. es rituali, garkveulwilad,

sruldeboda im mizniTac, rom gardacvlili ukan dabrunebisgan
yofiliyo daculi. am Cveulebidanac vlindeba saiqio arsebobis
rwmena pirvelyofil adamianebSi. aseve Zvel saflavebSi napovni
nivTebi naTlad miuTiTeben saiqio cxovrebis rwmenaze, radgan

Cayolebuli nivTi gardacvlils im qveynadac dasWirdeboda.

2. 2. primitiuli religiebi
a) animizmi
pirvelyofili adamianebis cxovrebis kvleviT dakavebuli
mecnierebi miuTiTeben animizmze (laT. “anima”, suli), rogorc
am drois adamianebis sulieri cxovrebis gansakuTrebul
Tvisebaze. TavisTavad animizmi ar warmoadgens religias. is
ufro Sexedulebaa garemomcvel samyaroze: bunebis movle­
naTa da sagnebis pirveladi axsna.
yvelaferi rasac veluri adamiani xedavs (ciuri movlenebi, mx­
ecebi, mcenareebi, qvebi da moSriale foTlebic ki) aRqmulia
mis mier iseTive cocxal da sulier arsebad, rogoric TviTon
aris. amrigad, yovel movlenasa da nivTs Tavisi suli (Anima)
aqvs. magram imisaTvis, rom velurma adamianma romelime sulis
Tayvaniscema daiwyos, saWiroa mocemulma nivTma an movlenam
gansakuTrebuli STabeWdileba moaxdinos masze. magaliTad,
rodesac amerikis velurma tomebma pirvelad naxes evropi­
dan maT miwaze Casuli cxeniani kaci, romelic cecxlsasroli
iaraRidan isroda, maT es arseba (cxenic da kacic, romelic er­
Tian qmnilebad CaTvales) quxilis RmerTad aRiqves.
amrigad, bunebis yvela movlenisa da nivTis “gansulierebiT”
veluris SegnebaSi mTeli samyaro boroti an keTili sulebiT
16

aris dasaxlebuli. isini ki ara mxolod garkveul cvlile­
bebs iwveven bunebaSi, aramed TviT adamianis bed-iRbalzec
did zegavlenas axdenen.
b) fetiSizmi
es termini momdinareobs franguli sitvisgan feticio, romelic
niSnavs amulets, Tilismas, xolo laTinuri factitius _ niSnavs
xelovnuri, gakeTebuli. rodesac portugalielebma pirvelad

3. werilobiTi wyaroebi
3. 1. Tanaxi (ebrauli biblia)
iudazimis wm. werilis saerTo saxelwodebaa Tanaxi, romelic
sami nawilisgan Sedgeba. saxelwodeba “Tanax” warmoadgens abre­
viaturas, Sedgenils am sami nawilis saxelwodebaTa pirveli
asoebisgan: T _ Tora (anu moses rjuli), n _ nabiim (winaswarme­
tyvelni), x _ qeTubim (werilni; “q” bgera “x”-d icvleba xmovnis
45

Semdeg). Tumca iudaizmis saxe gamokveTa mTelma wyebam wignebisa,
romlebic Tanaxis Semdgom Camoyalibda (maT Sesaxeb ix. qvemoT).
Tanaxis pirvel nawilSi Sedis Tora, anu moses xuTi wigni
(Sesaqme, gamosvlaTa, levitelTa, ricxvTa da meore rjulis
wignebi); meore nawilSi (nabiim) Sedis isu naves, msajulTa,
mefeTa da winaswarmetyvelTa wignebi; xolo mesame nawili
(qeTubim) moicavs daviTis fsalmunebs, igavnis, iobis qebaTa
qebas, ruTis, esTeris, eklesiastes da sxva wignebs.
„...dadebuli aRTqma da “rCeuli eris” gageba gulisxmobs imas,
rom ebraelebi uflis mier mowodebulni iyvnen kacobriobis
istoriaSi gansakuTrebuli misiis aRsrulebisTvis (...) gamos­
vlaTas wignis 24:7 muxlTan dakavSirebuli rabinistuli ko­
mentarebis Tanaxmad, Tora SeTavazebuli iqna mravali eris
mimarT, magram mxolod israelma miiRo igi”.
С. Пилкингтон. Иудаизм. М., 2002, 36-37

rogorc vxedavT, ebrauli bibliis anu Tanaxis ekvivalents qris­
tianul religiaSi warmoadgens Zveli aRTqma. magram gamoTqma
“Zveli aRTqma” ar gamoiyeneba iudevelTa mier. sityva aRTqma

3. 2. zepiri Tora: Talmudi
Talmudi iudaizmis literaturul-kanonikuri kompleqsis
krebiTi saxelia. sityva “Talmudi” momdinareobs ebrauli
fuZisgan “lameid”, rac niSnavs Seswavlas. Talmudi ori naw­
ilisgan Sedgeba, romelTac ewodebaT miSna da hemara.
rabinTa mtkicebiT, mosem uflisgan ori Tora miiRo _ erTi
werilobiTi, meore zepiri. es ukanaskneli zepiradve gadae­
cemoda Taobidan Tobas, sanam miSnaSi ar Caiwera (hemara mx­
olod miSnas komentarebia).
miSna ax. w. II-III ss-ebSi Camoyalibda. es sityva SeiZleba iTargm­
nos rogorc “gameoreba”. miSna moculobiT sakmaod didi kom­
pilaciaa e.w. “uxucesTa gadmocemebisa”, romlebSic aRwerilia
Tanaxis gmirebis, brZeni uxucesebis wes-Cveulebebis, maT Soris
mimdinare kamaTebisa da sxva ambebis Sesaxeb. miSna eqvsi ganyo­
filebisgan Sedgeba, romlebic sul 63 traqtats Seicavs.
miSnas CawerisTanave daiwyo mis debulebebTan dakavSire­
buli ganxilvebi, romelic saukuneebi gagrZelda. swored
am diskusiebis Sedegad Camoyalibda komentarebis krebuli,
romelsac hemara ewoda (ix. qvemoT).
Talmudi Seicavs dogmatur, samarTlebriv, religiur-filo­
sofiur Tu moraluri Sinaarsis kanonebsa da wesebs. Talmud­
is werilobiTi gaformeba ax. w. II s-Si daiwyo.
„miSnas Semdgeneli da redaqtori iyo rabini iehuda ha-nasi (ax. w.
135-217). mis Sesadgenad rabi iehudam gamoiyena miSnas ufro Zve­
li krebulebi (...) SemdgomSi iehudas mowafeebmac Seitanes masSi
garkveuli cvlilebebi da damatebebi. Cvenamde moRweulia mi­
Snas sami varianti: 1. sakuTriv calke gamocemuli miSna; 2. ieru­
salimuri Talmudis miSna da 3. babilonuri Talmudis miSna”.
Энциклопедия Иудаизма. Пер. с Иврита. Иерусалим, 1983,
статья: “Мишна”.

4. 2. locva

dRes aResruleba locva: dilas, SuadRiT da saRamos.

swavlebis Tanaxmad, wmindad iTvleba ara locvis adgili, ar­
amed locvis dro. locvebi aResruleba ebraul enaze, magram
Tu morwmunes ar SeuZlia Zvel ebraulad locvis kiTxva, neba­
darTulia uflis winaSe sakuTari sityvebiT locva, radgan
«axloa ufali yvela im adamianTan, vinc mas WeSmaritebiT
mouxmobs» (fsal. 144:18).
imisaTvis, rom sinagogaSi RvTismsaxureba daiwyos saWiroa
aranakleb 10 mamakaci (ara aqvs mniSvneloba ramdeni qalia am
dros sinagogaSi). locviTi Sekrebis winamZRvars uwodeben
xazans an kantors. Tumca koleqtiuri locvisTvis saWiroa
masSi TiToeuli mlocvelis aqtiuri monawileoba.

5. 3. sikvdilis Semdeg

6.1. aSkenazuri da sefaraduli iudaizmi
sxvadasxva garemoSi arsebul kulturul pirobebTan misad­
agebis procesSi rabinistuli civilizacia TandaTanobiT or

naparTa STamomavalni arian, romlebmac iudaizmi VIII s-Si
miiRes. aSkenazTa umravlesoba vaWari iyo. saubrobdnen

6. 2. Tanamedrove iudaizmis formireba
Sua saukuneebis rabinuli sistemis rRveva iwyeba XVII s-Si, jer
holandiaSi, Semdeg ki inglisSi. avstriasa da safrangeTSi is
XVIII s-is dasasruls iwyeba, evropis sxva qveynebSi ki mxolod
XIX s-Si. iudaizmis es kolafsi dakavSirebulia iudevelTa mier
mniSvnelovani individualuri uflebebis, zogierT SemTxveva­
Si ki sruli Tanasworuflebianobis mopovebiT. amgvari samarT­
lebrivi revolucia niSnavda ebrauli Temebis xelmZRvanelTa
(rabinTa) avtoritarul18 mmarTvelobis dasrulebas.
“ebraeli swavluli, israel Saxaki iudaizmis modernizacias
Semdegi sityvebiT aRwers: “damsxvreul iqna erT-erTi yvelaze
Caketili da totalitaruli sazogadoebis borkilebi. es gan­
Tavisufleba, iudaizmSi, ZiriTadad, garedan iyo Semosuli,
Tumca zogierTi ebraeli am process “Signidanac” exmarebo­
da. mravali saukunis Semdeg, pirvelad, ebraels SeuZlia imis
gakeTeba, rac mas surs, samoqalaqo uflebebis farglebSi, ra
Tqma unda. iudevelma miiRo ufleba da Tavisufleba swavlisa
da wignebis kiTxvisa Tanamedrove enebze, nebismieri sakvebis
miRebisa, seqsualur cxovrebasTan dakavSiebuli uamravi ab­
surduli akrZalvis ignorirebisa, sakuTari azris flobisac
ki da sxva. es yovelive evropis (da mogvianebiT sxva qveynebis)
ebraelebs axali drois wyobilebis wyalobiT miecaT”.
Г. Ястребов. Введение в Иудаизм. М., 2005, gv. 54

aqtiurad viTardeboda bibliuri teqstebisadmi kritiku­
li midgomis tendencia, romelic eWvis qveS ayenebda moses
avtorobas xuTwigneulTan (TorasTan) mimarTebaSi da sxv.
aseTma mdgomareobam ki TandaTan iudaizmis pluralizacia,
misi sxvadasxva mimarTulebebad daSla gamoiwvia. TiToeuli
maTgani cdilobda sakuTari pasuxi gaeca Tanamedroveobis
gamowvevebze.
amJamad iudaizmis ZiriTadi mimarTulebebi Semdegia: ultraor­
Todoqsia, orTodoqsia, konservatuli iudaizmi, reform­
istuli (liberaluri) iudaizmi da rekonstruqcionistuli
iudaizmi. yvelaze metad tradiciuli mimdinareoba iudaizmSi
ultraorTodoqsiaa, yvelaze liberaluri _ rekonstruqcion­
istuli iudaizmi. magram iudevelTa umravlesoba miekuTvneba
ara am ukidures mimdinareobebs, aramed orTodoqsalur, kon­

rols asrulebs aseve sekularuli iudaizmi, romelic, ZiriTa­
dad, ebrauli kulturis mniSvnelobaze akeTebs aqcents.

winaaRmdeg da rogorc mistikuri tradiciis gagrZeleba (“me­

6. 4. orTodoqsia
orTodoqsuli iudaizmi Camoyalibda XIX s-Si, rogorc reaq­
cia ganmanaTleblobis epoqis tendenciebis winaaRmdeg. am mim­
dinareobis mTavari damaxasiaTebeli niSani: biblia mxolod
RvTaebriv gamocxadebas Seicavs, romelSic ar aris adamianu­
ri mcdari msjelobebi (SedarebisTvis: qristianuli eklesia
ara mxolod Zveli, aramed axal aRTqmasTan mimarTebaSic aRi­
arebs mociqulTa pirovnuli, adamianuri azrebis arsebobas.
amaze miuTiTebs, magaliTad, TviT pavle mociqulis ramden­
ime gamoTqma: “amas vambob adamianuri msjelobiT” (rom. 3:5;
6:19; 1 kor. 9:8); “amas ki me geubnebiT da ara ufali” (1 kor.
7:12), zogierT sakiTxze ki pavle ambobda, rom maTze “ara
aqvs uflis brZaneba” (1 kor. 7:25). Tumca es garemoeba ufro
“rCeviTi” da “brZanebiT” xasiaTs gulisxmobs mociqulis si­
tyvebisa, vidre mis mcdarobasa Tu ucdomelobas, radgan sxva
adgilas pavle wers: “vfiqrob, rom mec maqvs suli RvTisa” (1
kor. 7:40). garda amisa qristem Tavis mociqulebs naTlad ga­
nucxada, rom misi amqveynidan wasvlis Semdgom maT suliwmin­
das mouvlenda, romelic “yvelafers gaswavliT da yvelafers
gagaxsenebT, rac TqvenTvis miTqvams” (ioan. 14:26). es sity­
vebi ki qristianuli religiis mixedviT, bibliis ucdomelo­
bis garantad miiCneva. Tumca am ucdomelobasac aqvs Tavisi
sazRvrebi, radgan is ar vrceldeba bibliis im monacemebze,
romlebic mecnierebis sxvadasxva dargebs ganekuTvneba (mag.,
zoologia, botanika, geografia, arqeologia, istoria...).
ucdomelad iTvleba bibliis is swavleba, romelic exeba ada­
mianisa da RmerTis urTierTobas, RvTis bunebas, religiurzneobriv swavlebas).

6. 5. konservatuli iudaizmi
konservatuli iudaizmi cdilobs SeinarCunos tradiciuli
iudaizmis arsebiTi elementebi, magram Tavis TavSi uSvebs
garkveul novaciebsac, Tumca ara iseTi gabeduli formebiT,

doqsias, SemoiRo ra rabinebad qalebis kurTxevis (xeldasxmis) wesi.
konservatuli iudaizmi gansakuTrebiT aSS-Sia gavrcelebuli. is­
raelSi konservatuli iudaizmis mimdevrebi TiTqmis ar arian.

6. 6. reformistuli (liberaluri) iudaizmi
reformistuli iudaizmi XIX s-is dasawyisSi germaniaSi iwyebs
Tavis ganviTarebas. igi aRiarebs sekularul filosofias da
Tvlis, rom iudauri tradicia Camoyalibebulia ara mxolod
RvTaebrivi gamocxadebis Sedegad, aramed aseve rogorc wmin­
dad adamianuri Zalisxmevis Sedegad da kulturuli garemoe­
bebis gavleniT. am mimdinareobas galaxis moTxovnebis dacva­
Si Setanili aqvs mniSvnelovani Serbilebebi, magaliTad, iTv­
leba, rom qaSruTis22 dacva pirovnuli arCevanis saqmea.
XIX s-is Sua wlebSi germaneli ebraelebis konservatizmis
gamo reformistuli iudaizmis ganviTareba Seferxda. Tum­
ca aSS-Si, piriqiT, es mimdinareoba ufro metad gaZlierda am
qveyanaSi iudeveli moazrovneebisa da rabinebis emigraciis
wyalobiT.

2. werilobiTi wyaroebi
2. 1. Zveli aRTqma
qristianul religiaSi Zveli da axali aRTqmis wignebis er­
Tobliobas biblia ewodeba. sityva «biblia» berZnulia da niSnavs
«wignebs» (mxolobiT ricxvSi «biblos»). rac Seexeba saxelwode­
bas «Zveli aRTqma», is pirvelive saukuneSi arsebobda. es gamoTq­
ma jer kidev pavle mociquls aqvs gamoyenebuli (2 kor. 3:14).
Zveli aRTqmis wignTa raodenoba (aqve avRniSnavT, rom wignebi
ewodeba ara mxolod Zvel aRTqmaSi Semaval wignebs, aramed ax­
ali aRTqmis epistoleebsac) sxvadasxva qristianuli eklesiis
gamocemul bibliaSi sxvadasxvaa. protestantuli eklesiebis
gamocemebSi masSi mxolod 38 wignia, xolo marTlmadideblur
da kaTolikur gamocemebSi garda am 38-isa, aris kidev 12 wigni.
am sxvaobis istoriuli mizezi is gaxlavT, rom Zveli aRTqmis
berZnuli Targmanis avtorebma Targmnes aseve is wignebic, rom­
lebsac ebraelebi ar miiCnevdnen kanonikurad. Zveli aRTqmis es
berZnuli Targmani cnobilia samocdaaTTa Targmanis (berZnu­
lad, septuaginta) saxelwodebiT, radgan gadmocemis Tanaxmad, igi
aleqsandriaSi iTargmna 70 (ufro zustad 72) mTargmnelis mier.
“ieso palestineli iudeveli iyo, romelic pirvel saukuneSi
cxovrobda. amitom Tanamedrove dasavleli adamianebisTvis
misi pirovneba da misi swavleba zogjer gaugebaria. Tumca
xSirad ise xdeba, rom Zalian advilia qristes sityvebis gage­
ba CvenTvis. am mxriv dasafasebelia, magaliTad, mark tvenis
mier naTqvami Semdegi sityvebi: “me maRelvebs ara is adgilebi
bibliaSi, romlebic ar mesmis, aramed is adgilebi, romlebic
sruliad gasagebia!”.
Джон Янг. Христианство. Пер с Англ., М., 2001, 16

2. 3. apokrifuli wignebi

bis or kategorias gamoyofen:
1. apokrifuli ewodeboda iseT wigns, romelic Tavisi Rrma
Sinaarsis gamo ar unda yofiliyo yvelasTvis anu rigiTi
adamianebisTvis wasakiTxi. aseTi saxis literatura mx­

ZloT maTi jerovani gageba.

li xasiaTis gamo, wm. eqvTime aTonelis termonilogiiT,
ewodeboda «natyuarni».

amgvari litaraturis warmoSobis mizezad miCneulia Semdegi
garemoeba: bibliaSi bevr rameze ar aris saubari, ris Sesaxebac
nebismieri adamiani isurvebda rom Seetyo. es SeuZlebelic aris,
radgan, rogorc ioane mociquli wers, iesos mier aRsrulebuli
yvela movlena, rom aRweriliyo, mTeli qveyanac ver daitevda
daweril wignebs (in. 21:25). biblia mxolod im WeSmaritebas Sei­
cavs, rac adamianis sulieri gadarCenisTvis aris aucilebeli.

3. 5. qorwinebis saidumlo
am saidumlos aRsrulebis dros axaldaqorwinebulni ieso
qristes winaSe samaradiso siyvarulisa da erTgulebis
dacvis pirobas deben. qristianuli eklesiis swavleba sak­
maod vrcel rCeva darigebebs moicavs col-qmruli urTier­
Tobebisa da bavSvebis aRzrdis sakiTxebTan dakavSirebiT.
qristianuli rwmenis mixedviT, qorwinebis saidumlos meS­
veobiT wyvilze gadmodis uflis gansakuTrebuli madli,
romelic maT exmareba cxovrebiseuli tvirTis erTad zid­

wineba ar mTavrdeba meuRleTa sikvdiliT, aramed maTi suli­
eri erToba uflis sasufevelSic grZeldeba. Tumca umTavres
saTnoebad RvTis winaSe mainc meuRleTa urTierTsiyvaruli
da pativiscema iTvleba da ara mxolod am ritualis gareg­
nuli aRsruleba.

3. 6. mRvdlobis saidumlo
gamorCeuli kandidatis sasuliero pirad (diakvnad, mRvdlad,

diakvnad da mRvdlad xeldasxma unda aRsruldes episkoposis mier,
xolo episkoposad xeldasxma aranakleb ori episkoposis mier.
marTlmadidebluri da kaTolikuri eklesiebis swavlebiT, ada­
mianis cxonebisTvis aucilebelia sasuliero pirTa Suamdgom­

bis absolutur umravlesobas ki dauSveblad miaCnia morwmunesa
da RmerTs Soris yovelgvari Suamavlis arseboba. maTi doqtrina
xSirad mRvdlobis sayovelTao principze miuTiTebs, romlis
Tanaxmadac qristes yvela morwmune iTvleba mRvdlad.

3. 7. zeTiscxebis saidumlo
es rituali saTaves iRebs mociqulTa droidan, romlebic
qristesgan miniWebuli ZaliT «mraval adamians aTavisuf­
lebdnen eSmakTagan da kurnavdnen maT zeTiscxebiT» (mark.
6:13). es saidumlo dRevandel eklesiaSic avadmyofi adamian­
isTvis aResruleba. ikiTxeba Sesabamisi locvebi da avadmy­
ofs specialurad am saidumlosTvis damzadebul zeTs usva­
men sxeulis im nawilze, romelic daavadebulia. iTvleba, rom
am dros avadmyofze uflis makurnebeli madli gadmodis,
romelic sxeulebrivi da aseve sulieri wylulebs kurnavs.
adreul eklesiaSi aseve saidumlod iTvleboda gardacvli­
lis damarxva da berad aRkveca. magaliTad, netari avgustine
(V s.) aRricxavda 13-mde saidumlos, romelTa Sorisac igi
moiazrebda marxvasac da pirjvris werasac.

“Tu ar moiqceviT da ar iqnebiT, rogorc bavSvebi, ver
SexvalT caTa sasufevelSi, radgan vinc daimdablebs Tavs,
rogorc es umciresi, igi udidesi iqneba caTa sasufevelSi”.

arafrisgan. swored am aqtSi vlindeba RvTis erT-erTi Tvise­

ba _ yovladZliereba, radgan Cven adamianebs imisaTvis rom

velgvari winaswar arsebuli masalis gareSe _ arafrisgan Se­
qmna samyaro, romlis ukidures zRvars jer kidev ver miaRwia

yve-biT _ RmerTkaci.

aRmosavleTis mTels saqristianos zogjer romis papis CaTv­
liTac. es gansakuTrebiT mexuTe msoflio krebaze gamoCnda,

qvemoT warmodgenil pasaJebSi).

4. 4. kacobriobis gamoxsna
qristianuli swavlebis Tanaxmad, vinaidan kacobriobaSi cod­
va erTi adamianis (adamis) mier Semovida, kacobriobis xsna
aseve erTi adamianis mier unda ganxorcielebuliyo (amitom
iwodeba ieso qriste xSirad meore adamad qristianul liter­
aturaSi). magram ieso rom mxolod adamiani yofiliyo, igi ver
SeZlebda kacobriobis codvebis sakuTar Tavze aRebas. misi
sikvdili ar iqneboda sakmarisi sasyideli mTeli qveynierebis
codvebisTvis (1 in. 2:2). mxolod RmerTs SeuZlia sikvdili xs­
nis iaraRad gamoiyenos. amisaTvis saWiro iyo RmerTi adamianad
qceuliyo, radgan RmerTs ar SeuZlia sikvdili. amitom RvTis
gankacebis saidumlo igive xsnis saidumloa. es aris qristian­
obis ZiriTadi ganmasxvavebeli niSani sxva religiebisgan.
“biwiereba ar aris iseTi Zlieri, rom keTili Zalis daZleva
SeeZlos da Cveni bunebis ugunureba ar aris RvTaebriv sibrZn­

4. 5. xatebis Tayvaniscema
qristianuli eklesiis kidev erT mniSvnelovan swavlebas war­
moadgens meSvide msoflio saeklesio krebaze miRebuli dadge­
nileba xatebis Tayvaniscemis Sesaxeb. xati (berZ. «eikon» _ “ga­
mosaxuleba”, “xateba”) es aris wmindanTa da eklesiis istoriis
143

mniSvnelovan, sakralur movlenaTa gamosaxuleba sxadasxva
saxis myar zedapirze, romelzec arsebobs Sesabamisi warwera.
kaTolikuri da marTlmadideblur eklesiebSi damkvid­
rebulia xatebis Tayvaniscema. xatze SeiZleba iyos gamosax­
uli rogorc pirovnebebi (qriste, mariami an romelime wmind­
ani) aseve qristes cxovrebidan romelime movlena (aRdgoma,
amaRleba, feriscvaleba da sxv.).

tianul eklesiaSi adreuli periodidanve ganviTarda wmindanTa
kultic. wmindanebad moixseniebian is adamianebi, romlebmac
Tavisi gansakuTrebuli zneobrivi siwmindiTa da religiuri moR­
vaweobis gamo uflis gansakuTrebuli madli miiRes. qristianebs
swamT, rom wmindanebi Suamdgomloben ufalsa da codvil kaco­
briobas Soris. wminda moRvaweebad miiCnevian ZiriTadad asketuri
wesiT mcxovrebi adamianebi. Tumca eklesia zogjer im adamianebis
kanonizaciasac57 axdens, romlebic marTalia ar iyvnen sasuliero
pirebi, Tumca gansakuTrebuli wvlili Seitanes sakuTari eris
cxovrebaSi (saqarTvelos marTlmadidebelma eklesiam aseTebad
miiCnia magaliTad, ilia WavWavaZe, eqvTime TayaiSvili da sxv).
«avgarozma, edeselTa qalaqis mefem, mxatvari miav­
lina, rom mas uflis xatis msgavseba gamoesaxa, magram

sakuTar cxovelmyofel pirisaxes zed daado samoseli,
gadabeWda samosze Tavisi gamoxatuleba da ase gaugza­
vna igi amis mosurne avgarozs».

4. 7. borotebis warmoSoba
wm. werilis Tanaxmad, angelozuri (uxilavi) samyaros Seqmnis Sem­
deg, sanam Cveni xiluli samyaro Seiqmneboda, adgili hqonda gran­

da. amis gamo isini zecidan iqnen gandevnili, ris Semdegac isini
yovelgvari siwmindisa da sikeTis moZuleebad iqcnen. angeloz­

ofeboda uflis brwyinvalebasa da didebasTan). am angelozebs
sxvadasxva saxeliT moixsenieben: demoni, satana, eSmaki.

sulebad. ufalma nebis Tavisufleba mianiWa gonier arse­
bebs (angelozebsa da adamianebs), raTa TiToeulma maTganma
sikeTeSi sakuTari Tavis gamowrTobiT mTeli Tavisi arsebiT

ubralod aRar SeuZlia, ufro swored, aRar surs borote­
bis Cadena (Tumca ki, Tavisufali nebis ZaliT, kvlav SeuZlia
borotebisken gadaxra).

4. 8. esqatologiuri swavleba

Tu indiferentuli damokidebuleba sxva adamianis mimarT.

da moxvediT CemTan...»

4. 9. damokidebuleba sxva religiebisadmi
rogoria qristianuli eklesiis damokidebuleba misi sazRvreb­
is miRma myofi adamianebis mimarT (iqnebian isini warmarTebi Tu
sxva religiis mimdevrebi)? jer kidev Zveli aRTqma miuTiTebs
im adamianebze, romlebic rCeuli eris miRma imyofebodnen,
Tumca RvTismoSiS ebraelebze aranaklebad mosawonni iyvnen
uflisTvis. aseTebi iyvnen, mag., iobi (ix. biblia, wigni iobisa
1:1); melqisedeki, romelsac mociquli pavle uwodebs RvTis Zis
msgavss da maradiul mRvdels (ebr. 7:3); iaTori, midiameli (e. i.
araiudeveli) mRvdeli, moses simamri (gamos. 2:16) da sxva.
pavle mociquli brZanebs, rom warmarTebs sakuTari sindisis
moTxovnebis dacviT SeuZliaT gadarCena da uflis wyalobis
miReba. imis gamo, rom iudevelTa msgavsad, dawerili rjuli
ar hqondaT warmarTebs, mociqulis mier “bunebiT rjulad”
wodebuli sindisi Tavad maT bunebaSi Cado RmerTma: “roca
warmarTni, romelTac rjuli ar gaaCniaT, bunebiTi rjulis
mixedviT cxovroben, Tumca rjuli ara aqvT, TavianTi Tavis
rjuli arian. isini aCveneben, rom rjulis saqme gulebSi uwe­
riaT, rasac mowmobs maTi sindisi da azrebi” (rom. 2:14).
”...warmarTebs, ramdenadac maTTvis aRsareba ucnobi iyo, aseTi wesi
hqondaT: gadiodnen zRvis sanapiroze, TavianT codvebs zRvis tal­
Rebs uyvebodnen da swamdaT, rom talRebi maT codvebs waiRebda”.

5. mimdinareobebi qristianobaSi
amJamad qristianoba ramdenime mimarTulebad aris dayofi­
li. amaTgan eklesiaTa xuTi mTavari jgufi SeiZleba gamoiy­
os: marTlmadidebluri, kaTolikuri, protestantuli, e. w.
nestorianuli da monofizituri eklesiebi.
am dayofilobis mizeziT, qristianobis, rogorc erTiani re­
ligiis doqtrinis, kultisa da organizaciuli mowyobis Ses­
axeb saubari sakmaod did siZneles warmoadgens. Tumca arsebobs
garkveuli principebi da niSan-Tvisebebi, romelic saerToa
yvela qristianuli eklesiisTvis. dogmatikaSi amgvar saerTo
princips warmoadgens wm. samebis Sesaxeb swavleba, romelsac
yvela qristianuli eklesia aRiarebs zogierTi marginaluri
protestantuli mimdinareobebis garda (ix. qvemoT).
agreTve TiTqmis yvela qristianuli eklesia aRiarebs
qristes, rogorc kacobriobis codvebis gamomsyidvels
jvarze gaRebuli msxverpliT. aseve qristes aRdgomasa da
sulis ukvdavebas.

bis (sakramentebis) aRsruleba. Tumca, rogorc zemoT aRini­

Sna, saidumloebebTan dakavSirebiT qristianul eklesiaTa

5. 1. aRmosavleTis marTlmadidebeli
eklesia

qalkedonis msoflio krebaze Camoyalibebuli qristologiuri
dogmatis miRebis Semdeg sakuTar Tavs «marTlmadidebels»
(berZ. «orTodoqsos») uwodebda im eklesiebis sapirispirod,

monofizituri eklesiebi). magram 1054 wlis ganxeTqilebis Semdeg,

saxuro teqstebSi zogjer kaTolikuri eklesiac marTlmadidebe­
lad iwodeba. da piriqiT, marTlmadidebeli eklesiac oficialu­

izebuli mmarTveloba. adgilobrivi eklesiebi mTlianad da­

flebiania, miuxedavad imisa Tu rogor iwodeba mocemuli
eklesiis saWeTmpyrobeli: patriarqad, kaTolikosad, mitro­
politad Tu arqiepiskoposad.

meZvelweseebi (staroverebi)

ganxeTqilebis mizezi ki im saeklesio reformis miuRebloba

ZiriTadad, veneciaSi da italiis sxva qalaqebSi ibeWdeboda.

1. 2. araqalkedonuri eklesiebi
a) nestorianoba
am eklesiis damfuZneblad miCneulia konstantinepolis pa­
triarqi nestori, romelic patriarqis taxtze 428-431 wlebSi
imyofeboda. gavrcelebuli azris Tanaxmad, nestorianelebi
Tvlidnen, rom ieso qriste iSva rogorc Cveulebrivi adami­
ani _ ieso qriste, masSi mxolod Semdeg Casaxlda Ze RmerTi.
gamodioda, rom qristeSi arsebobda rogorc Ze RvTisa, aseve
Ze kacisa. amave mizeziT isini mariams uwodebdnen ara RvTis
mSobels, aramed qristes (adamianis) mSobels.
mesame msoflio saeklesio krebaze (efeso, 431 weli) nesto­
rianizmis saxeliT cnobili swavleba eresad (mwvaleblobad)
gamocxadda. Tumca dRes bolomde garkveuli ar aris, mar­
Tla amgvar Sexedulebebs gamoTqvamda sakuTriv patriarqi
nestori Tu misi Sexedulebebi arasworad gadmosces, an isini
realurad sxvas ekuTvnoda, radgan mis pirad nawerebSi aRmo­
Cenilia sruliad orTodoqsuli Sexedulebebi am sakiTxze.
msgavsi Tvalsazrisi sakmaod damajereblad gamoTqves dasav­
lelma mecnierebma (maT Soris yvelaze cnobili, kembrijis
universitetis profesori, beTiun bekeria). msgavsi Sexed­
ulebebia aseve gamoTqmuli ramdenime rusuli warmoSobis
sakmaod kompetenturi istorikosisa Tu bizantologis naS­
romSic (ix., mag., posnovis (gv. 377-401), kartaSevis (gv. 293323) da meiendorfis (gv. 180) wignebi amave saxelmZRvaneloSi
«qristianobis» bolos CamoTvlil literaturaSi).
asea Tu ise, es eklesia am droidan (V s.) nestorianul ekle­
siad iwodeboda da am eretikul swavlebasac nestorianizmis
saxeli daerqva.

172

b) monofizitoba
rogorc miCneulia, aRmosavleTis zogierT eklesias amgvari
saxeli (monofizituri) ewodaT maT mier 451 wels qalkedonSi
Catarebuli meoTxe msoflio saeklesio krebis dadgenilebis
uaryofis gamo. am dadgenilebis (dogmatis) mixedviT qristes
ori _ RvTaebrivi da adamianuri buneba hqonda (berZ. «dio»
_ ori, «fizis» _ buneba). maT, diofizituris sapirisp­
irod, monofizit qristianebsac uwodebdnen (berZ. «mono»
_ erTi). Tumca dRes maT negatiuri damokidebuleba aqvT am
zedwodebis (monofizituri) mimarT da sakuTar Tavs moix­
senieben an marTlmadidebel an samociqulo eklesiad (mag.,
somxuri samociqulo eklesia).
monofizitTa umravlesoba ufro metad qristes RvTaebriv
bunebas usvamdnen xazs, vidre adamianurs, Tumca srulebiT ar
uaryofdnen qristeSi adamianuri bunebis arsebobasac. amitom

5. 3. adreuli protestantuli eklesiebi
qristianobaSi protestantuli mimdinareoba yvelaze bolos
warmoiSva (pirveli oTxi ZiriTadi ganayofis Semdgom). XVI
s-Si evropis sxvadasxva qveyanaSi reformaciis procesi dai­
wyo, rodesac ramdenime qristianulma eklesiam uaryo kaTo­
likuri eklesiis doqtrinaluri, sakulto da organizaciul
mmarTvelobasTan dakavSirebuli sakiTxebi. amgvarad, am ek­
lesiaTa krebiTi saxeli gaxlavT «protestantizmi» evropis
dominanti (romis kaTolikuri) eklesiis winaaRmdeg gamoTq­
muli protestis Sesabamisad.
amrigad, protestantizmi warmoiSva ara rogorc erTi konk­
retuli aRmsarebloba, aramed sxvadasxva adgilas warmoqm­
nil mimdinareobaTa da moZraobaTa erToblioba. am prot­
estantul jgufebs Soris ki, arsebobda rogorc gansxvave­
bebi, aseve msgavsebebi. upirvelesad aRsaniSni garemoeba is
gaxlavT, rom protestantizmi aRiarebs bibliis uzenaes av­
toritets rogorc rwmenis fundaments (gansxvavebiT kaTo­
likuri eklesiisgan, romelic uzenaes avtoritetad da msof­
lios msajulad romis paps aRiarebda).
rac Seexeba wm. gadmocemas, mas protestantebi, rogorc wesi,
ar aRiareben. aseve zogadi protestantuli principis Tanax­
mad, adamianis cxoneba SesaZlebelia mxolod uflis mimarT
piradi rwmeniT da ara samRvdeloebis daxmarebiT. protes­
tantebs ar swamT wmindanTa Suamdgomlobisa uflis winaSe. am
mizeziT isini ar aRiareben xatebis Tayvaniscemis praqtikas.

aRiarebs mxolod or saidumlos: naTlobasa da ziarebas, radgan
maTi mtkicebiT, axal aRTqmaSi mxolod am ori saidumlos aR­

luTeris sikvdilis Semdeg eklesiis reformis process kal­
vini (1509-1564) Caudga saTaveSi. kalvinizmis ZiriTadi doqtri­
naluri debulebebi sxvadasxva variaciebiT mocemulia ramden­

vestminsterul (1647 w. da sxva aRmsareblobebSi. kalvinizmis
yvelaze metad damaxasiaTebelia swavleba winaswargansazRvru­
lobis Sesaxeb, romlis Tanaxmad, RmerTma jer kidev samyaros
Seqmnamde winaswar gansazRvra adamianTa erTi nawili gadasar­
Cenad, meore ki dasaRupad (Tumca mogvianebiT zomierma kalvin­
istebma cota Searbiles es swavleba). magram ramdenadac uflis
sibrZne miuwvdomelia, aravis SeuZlia icodes sakuTari xvedri.
adamianma unda aRasrulos keTili saqmeebi, magram es kalvi­
nizmSi ganixileba ara adamianis cxonebis saSualebad, aramed
imis niSnad, rom igi uflisgan aris gamorCeuli. aseve kalvin­
isturi swavlebiT, amqveyniuri materialuri keTildReoba
aSkara niSania adamianis uflisgan kurTxeulobisa.
kalvinis swavlebiT, evqaristiuli saidumlos dros purSi
da RvinoSi qriste realurad myofobs, oRond ara fizikurad
(xorcisa da sisxlis saxiT) aramed sulierad, uxilavad.
kalvinisti sasuliero pirebi ar gansxvavdebian SesamosliT
eriskacebisgan. maT taZrebSi arc xatebia da arc ferweris
nimuSebi. RvTismsaxurebis dros ar anTeben sanTlebs.

am sami mimdinareobis doqtrina TiTqmis erTi da igivea.

ramdenime aTeuli adamiani, magram aman seriozulad SeaS­

dan muqaraze da muhamedis pirveli mimdevrebis devnaze ga­
davidnen. amrigad, muhamedis mravali mimdevari ukve 615 w.
iZulebuli iyo, TavSesafari qristianul eTiopiaSi eZebna.

da, radgan igi sakuTari biZis mfarvelobis qveS imyofeboda,
romelic maSin gvaris meTaurad iTvleboda.
«[arabi] vaWrebis es fena garda qonebis daunjebisa, araferze
fiqrobda. religia da sarwmunoeba maTTvis mxolod saqmeSi
warmatebis miRwevis saSualeba iyo. Tu islamis qadageba maT

4. 1. islamis xuTi WeSmariteba
yuranisa da sunas Tanaxmad yvela muslimi valdebulia, aRi­
aros rwmenis xuTi dogmati: a) erTi RmerTis rwmena; b) an­

ciqulTa rwmena; e) gankiTxvis dRis rwmena.
a) erTi RmerTis rwmena
islamSi rwmenis upirveles sagans RmerTis erTaderToba war­
moadgens (monoTeizmi). yuranSi, msgavsad bibliisa, RmerTi
warmodgenilia, erTi mxriv, rogorc yovlisSemZle da mrisx­
ane, meores mxriv ki _ rogorc mowyale da mosiyvarule ar­
seba. RmerTi Tavisi arsiT miuwvdomelia, magram igi Tavad au­
wyebs adamianebs sakuTar nebas gamocxadebis meSveobiT.
yuranSi xSirad aris saubari imis Sesaxeb, rom samyaro RvTis
mier aris Seqmnili. Tumca, ar aris gadmocemuli sistematuri
Txroba Sesaqmis (samyaros Seqmnis) Sesaxeb, rogorc amas, ma­
galiTad, bibliis pirvel wignSi vxvdebiT. aRniSnul sakiTxze
yuraniseuli Txroba garkveul nawilebSi emTxveva bibliur
Txrobas, zogierT nawilSi ki isini mniSvnelovnad gansxvavde­
bian erTmaneTisgan.
yuranis mixedviT adamiani uflis rCeuli qmnilebaa, is misi
monacvlea dedamiwaze. magram swored imis gamo, rom igi
RvTis qmnilebaa, adamiani RmerTze damokidebuli arsebaa,
romlisganac ganuwyvetliv Rebulobs sasicocxlo Zalebs
(rogorc suliers, aseve fizikurs). marTalia yurani ar sau­
brobs RvTis mier adamianis Tavis xatad da msgavsad Seqmnis

muhamedis gardacvalebis Semdeg dadga sakiTxi, Tu vin unda

magram qalaq medinis mosaxleobis erTma jgufma ar aRiara

Siitebi ewodebaT.
SiitTa azriT, xalifas daniSvnis dros memkvidreobiTobis
princips unda miniWeboda upiratesoba, magram morwmuneTa
umravlesobis azriT, xalifebi pirovnuli Rirsebebis mixed­

principiT iqna gamorCeuli pirveli sami xalifa: abu beqri,
omari da osmani. rodesac meoTxe xalifas arCevis dro mov­
ida, Siitebma Tavis mizans miaRwies da ali gamoacxades xal­
ifad, magram 661 w. am or partias Soris mimdinare sisxlism­
Rvreli omis dros, ali mokles. ali mowamed gamoacxades da
iqve dakrZales. es saflavi (q. najafi) SiitTaTvis dRemde
wminda adgilia.
am mkvlelobis Semdeg muslimuri samyaro or nawilad gaiyo:
sunitebad da Siitebad. sunitebi (sruli saxelwodebiT, “sunas
xalxi”) warsulSic da dResac umravlesobaSi arian. aRiareben
oTxive xalifis mmarTvelobis legitimurobas, romlebsac
236

«marTal (marTlmorwmune) xalifebad» moixsenieben. Siitebi
ki ukanonod miiCneven pirveli sami xalifis mmarTvelobas. Si­
itebma ar irwmunes sunas is versia, romelic pirveli sami xal­
ifis momxreebma Camoayalibes. maT sakuTari suna SeimuSaves,
romelsac arabulad «bida» _ «siaxle» ewodeba.
Siitebi mxolod xalifa alis da misi STamomavali imamebis
xelisuflebis kanonierebas aRiareben, magram SemdgomSi Si­
itebs Sorisac moxda Sida ganxeTqileba. maTi azri gaiyo imas­
Tan dakavSirebiT, Tu alis romeli STamomavlebi unda mieCni­
aT uflebamosil imamebad. erTi nawili aseTad mxolod Svid
imams aRiarebs, meore nawili ki Tormets.
amrigad, religiuri ganxeTqileba islamSi Tavdapirvelad
ganpirobebuli iyo politikuri mizeziT, romelic saxali­
fos politikuri Zalauflebis kanonierebasTan dakavSire­
bulma polemikam gamoiwvia. Tumca am dapirispirebam Tanda­
TanobiT religiuri ganzomileba SeiZina.
sunitebi Tanamedrove muslimuri samyaros 84%-s Seadgenen,
Siitebi ki 16%-s. Siitebi umravlesobaSi sam qveyanaSi arian
_ iranSi, azerbaijansa da eraySi. yvela danarCen muslimur
qveyanaSi isini umciresobaSi arian.

5. 2. vahabizmi
vahabizmi _ es aris religiur-politikuri mimdinareoba
sunitur islamSi. aRmocenda me-18 saukuneSi, centralur

7. islami saqarTveloSi
saqarTveloSi islami Semovida arabebis batonobis periodSi
(VII-IX ss.). rodesac me-7 saukunis Sua xanebSi arabma sardalma
habib ibn maslama al-fihrim daipyro somxeTi da qarTl-kaxeTi.
man Tbiliss «dacvis sigeli» gadasca, rac gulisxmobda zavis
dadebas. qarTvelebma srul ganadgurebas amjobines uomrad,
winaaRmdegobis gareSe morCileba. sigelis Tanaxmad qarTve­
lebs xarki (jizia) unda exadaT arabebisTvis, magram vinc mus­
limur sarwmunoebas aRiarebda, is Tavisufldeboda xarkis­
gan. Zveli islamuri tradiciis Tanaxmad, muslimTa laSqrobis
dros warmarTebis (arab. «muSrikun») moqceva savaldebulo
iyo, iudevelebisa da qristianebis (arab. «ahl al-qiTab», rac
niSnavs «wm. werilis xalxs») gamuslimeba ki ar miiCneoda auci­
leblad, Tuki isini Tavs muslimi xelmwifis qveSevrdomad aRi­
arebdnen da gadasaxads gadaixdidnen. Tumca, gamuslimeba ar
gulisxmobda Zalmomreobas, radgan yurani naTlad acxadebs:
«aranairi iZuleba sarwmunoebaSi!» (yurani 2:257).

na moaxdina aseve brahmanizmidan (ix. qvemoT) warmoSobil in­
duizmze, Tumca Semdgom budizmi swored induizmma gandevna
indoeTidan da XII s-Si es religia ukve praqtikulad aRar ar­
sebobda am qveyanaSi.
ax. w. I saukunisTvis budizmi ukve or mTavar mimdinareobad
aris dayofili. maTi saxelwodebebia hinaiana da mahaiana (ix.).
mTeli Tavisi arsebobis manZilze budizmma Seqmna da ganavi­

naTlebis sistemac ki _ sxva sityvebiT, mTeli civilizacia.

2. budizmis werilobiTi wyaroebi
2. 1. tripitaka
budisturi swavlebis ZiriTadi debulebebi gadmocemulia e. w.
kanonikur literaturaSi. maTSi dafiqsirebulia Tavad budas
qadagebebi da gamocxadebebi, romelic SemdgomSi misi mowafee­
255

bis mier Caiwera. masSivea ganTavsebuli budisturi dogmebis,
wes-Cveulebebisa da moraluri principebis axsna-ganmartebebi.
es literatura cnobilia saxelwodebiT “tripitaka”, rac si­
tyvasityviT niSnavs “sammag kalaTas”, ufro xSirad ki iTarg­
mneba rogorc “kanonTa sami kalaTa”. gadmocemis mixedviT,
budas gardacvalebis Semdeg, misi mimdevari berebi erTad
Seikribnen da budas uaxloesi mowafeebis mowmobebi mois­
mines imasTan dakavSirebiT Tu rogori iyo budas swavlebis
ZiriTadi principebi. erTma budas mier gamoTqmuli is princ­
ipebi gadmosca, romlebic berTa cxovrebis wes-gangebas ex­
eba. meorem sakuTriv religiuri moZRvreba, romelic budas
mier saubrebisa da igavebis formiT iyo gadmocemuli. mesamem
ki maswavleblis filosofiuri xasiaTis msjelobebi gaixsena.
swored am mizeziT daiyo misi swavleba sam nawilad: (1) «ka­
laTa wesdebisa», romelSic Cawerilia disciplinaruli wese­
bi berebisTvis, (2) «kalaTa swavla-moZRvrebisa», romelSic
Cawerilia budas qadagebebi da gamonaTqvamebi; (3) «kalaTa
komentarebisa», romelic Seicavs axsna-ganmartebebs budis­
turi filosofiuri debulebebisa da zogadad doqtrinisa.
tripitakaSi Semavali swavleba saukuneebis ganmavlobaSi gan­
icdida formirebas, sanam igi saboloo saxiT Camoyalibde­
boda. igi Tavdapirvelad zepiri gziT gadaecemoda Taobidan
Taobas. es swavleba pirvelad Caweril iqna palis enaze Zv. w. I
s-Si ceilonis kunZulze (Sri-lanka). mogvianebiT ki sxvadasx­
va budisturma skolam da mimdinareobam tripitakis bevri
adgili Secvala da gadaakeTa. amitom 1871 wels mandalaSi
(birma) moiwvies saerTo budisturi kreba, sadac 2,400-ma bud­
istma berma sxvadasxva xelnawerisa da Targmanis SejerebiT
erTiani, unificirebuli tripitakis teqsti Camoayaliba. es
teqsti amokveTes 729 marmarilos filaze, romelTagan Ti­
256

Toeuli moaTavses calkeul miniaturul taZarSi. amrigad,
Seiqmna patara qalaqi-biblioTeka, saxelwodebiT kutodo.
mas Semdeg es qalaqi budistebis Tayvaniscemis adgilia.

2. 2. sutrebis kalaTa
garda tripitakisa, arsebobs sxva budisturi teqstebic. maTi
krebiTi saxelia “sutrebis94 kalaTa”, romelic xuT nawilad
iyofa. TiToeul am nawilSi sxvadasxva zomis teqstebi Sedis
da isini aucileblad Semdegi sityvebiT iwyeba: “ase movismine
me...”. am frazas miaweren anandas, budas sayvarel mowafes,
romelmac budas nirvanaSi gadasvlis Semdgom moZRvris qad­
agebebi pirvelad Catarebul budistur krebaze gaixsena.
zogierTma sutram didi popularoba moixveWa da Sesabamisad
maTze mravali ganmarteba daiwera. aseTia, magaliTad, “alma­
sis sutra”, romelmac samxreT-aRmosavleT aziis budistebze
didi gavlena moaxdina. es sutra mowmobs, rom am samyaroSi
yvelaferi aris maia95, anu iluzorulia da ararealuri. amis
gacnobierebiT ki SesaZlebelia “sicarielis, gandgomilebisa
da simSvidis” SenarCuneba.
CineTsa da iaponiaSi popularulia “uzenaesi kanonis lo­
tosis sutra”. masSi saubaria budas transcendenturobis
(miRmurobis) Sesaxeb, radgan igi warmodgenilia ara rogorc
istoriuli pirovneba, aramed mTlianad samyaros arsad. am
sutras budizmis am qveynebSi gavrcelebuli mimdinarebis _
mahaianas saxelmZRvanelosac uwodeben. am sutraSi aseve wina
planzea wamoweuli rwmena sayovelTao (yvela adamianis) ga­
darCenis SesaZleblobis Sesaxeb.

3. religiuri praqtika
3. 1. budisti berebis cxovrebis wesi
budisturi wyaroebis Tanaxmad, budizms mxari dauWires kSa­
triebma (meomrebma), vaiSebma (vaWrebma) da qalaqis mmarTve­
lebma, radgan maT am axali religiis qadagebaSi brahmanTa
batonobisgan ganTavisuflebis SesaZlebloba dainaxes. ada­
mianTa TanasworobasTan, keTilsindisier mmarTvelobasTan
da moTminebasTan dakavSirebulma budisturma ideebma mniS­
vnelovnad Seuwyo xeli mis popularobas.
budizmi gansakuTrebuli simpaTiiT ganimsWvala indoeTis
imperatori aSoka (Zv. w. III s.). misi xelSewyobiT budizmi ara
mxolod indoeTis oficialur religiad gamocxadda, aramed
mis sazRvrebsac gascda.
budizmis zneobrivi da socialuri ideebi mimzidveli aRmoC­
nda mTlianad sazogadoebisTvisac (ix. qvemoT pasaJi). rac Se­
exeba nirvanas misaRwevad SemuSavebul praqtikas: is mxolod
am qveynisgan gandgomil berTa Soris iyo gavrcelebuli. ami­
tom pirveli budisturi Temebi, am sityvis mkacri gagebiT,
ber-monazonTa Temebi iyo.

bis moxdenis SesaZleblobiT gansxvavdeboda karmis budisturi

zogadad sakvebis miRebisas mkacri TavSekavebiT.
am rvasafexuriani gzis gavlisa da miwieri arsebobis survi­
lis daZlevis meSveobiT SesaZlebelia xelaxali dabadebe­
bisgan (reinkarnacia) Semdgari jaWvis garRveva, anu sansaris
wrebrunvidan gaRweva da umaRlesi mdgoma-reobis, nirvanis

gansazRvruli (ix. qvemoT). naTelia mxolod is, rom es mdgo­
mareoba CvenTvis gaurkveveli da eniT aRuwerelia. mas Tan­
daTanobiT igeben mxolod is adamianebi, romlebic sulieri
ganviTarebis saboloo safexu-ramde aRweven. nirvana es erT­
droulad tanjvisgan ganTavisuf-lebuli gonebis netari
mdgomareoba da arayofierSi gadasvlaa.

4.3. dharma, nacvlad Semoqmedi RmerTisa

rvasafexuriani srulyofilebisa da gasxivosnebis gzis gav­
lac azrsmoklebulia da ewinaaRmdegeba karmis kanonsa da
budizmis sxva doqtrinalur debulebebs.

5. 1. hinaiana
hinaiana _ viwro gza (gadarCenisa). budizmis orTodoqsul

mas zogjer samxreTul budizmzsac uwodeben (gavrcele­

sxvadasxva dros ganxorcielebuli xuTasze meti reinkarnaciis
Semdeg miaRwia. igi meoTxe budad iTvleba mimdinare (amJamind­
el) sansaraSi. mis garda, kidev 20 buda arsebobda wina sansareb­
Si. buda maSin evlineba samyaros, rodesac kacobrioba sulierzneobriv ufskruls uaxlovdeba. maTi funqciaa kacobriobas
sibnelidan da cdomilebidan amosasvleli gza miuTiTon.
ornaxevari aTaswleulis Semdgom qveynierebas kvlav axali
buda moevlineba saxelad maitreia. igi ukanaskneli buda
iqneba mimdinare sansaraSi. hinaianas swavlebiT, danarCen ad­
amianebs SeuZliaT nirvanis miRweva, magram yvelas ar ZaluZs

5. 5. Zen-budizmi
es mimarTuleba Camoyalibda CineTSi ax. w. VI s-Si, SeiTvisa ra Cinuri kulturis mravali elementi. Zen-budizmi ar
ganasxvavebs erTmaneTisgan sansarasa da nirvanas. misi swav­
lebiT gasxivosnebis miRweva SesaZlebelia saero cxovre­
bis pirobebSic, gansakuTrebuli monastruli garemos gare­

wavleblisgan moswavles.

li popularoba moipova Can-budizmis (Cinurad), anu Zenbudizmis (iaponurad) mimarTulebam.

mniSvnelobas ar aniWebs logikur, gonebismier azrovnebas.

qcia ekisreba, magram mas adamianis WeSmaritebamde miyvana ar
SeuZlia. Zen budizmi mniSvnelovnad miiCnevs mxolod “wminda
gamocdilebasa” da “umaRles intuicias”.

5. mimdinareobebi induizmSi
5. 1. Sivaizmi
induizmi gayofilia Sivaizmad da viSnuizmad, romlebic Sesa­

Sivas kulti sakmaod winaaRmdegobrivia. igi aRiqmeba rogorc
damsjel da damangrevel Zalad (mas xSirad sikvdilis RmerTsac
uwodeben), magram igi imavdroulad Semoqmed da macocxlebel
RvTaebadac iTvleba. SivaSi erTdroulad aris gaerTianebuli
rogorc keTili, aseve boroti sawyisi. Sivas meuRles ewodeba
qalRmerTi kali, romelic demonTa mbrZaneblad iTvleba. mas
SeuZlia demonebs aukrZalos an ubrZanos sxvadasxva saxis ube­
durebebis, katastrofebis, epidemiebis movlena dedamiwaze.
RvTaeba kalis kulti gavrcelebulia indoeTis teritoriis
udides nawilSi. mas gansakuTrebiT qalebi scemen Tayvans. Si­
vaizmi Tavis mxriv iyofa Saktizmad, vamaCarizmad da a.S.

1. konfucianoba
konfuci _ es aris laTinizirebuli forma Cinuri saxelisa “kun

gaxldaT cnobili Cineli moazrovne konfuci. igi daibada mx­

igi 13 wlis ganmavlobaSi mogzauribs qveyanaSi, dadis sofelsofel da qadagebs Tavis sibrZnes, adamianebs mouwodebs
ufro meti humanurobis dacvisken. mis mier SemuSavebuli

iyo sakmaod konservatuli xasiaTisa. misi swavleba arsebuli
eTikuri normebis keTilsindisier dacvas gulisxmobda.
